<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перенять.html>переня́ть</a> (16405)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нять</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-njatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перенять.html>переня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perenjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перенимать.html>перенима́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to adopt, to imitate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перенять.html>переня́ть</a></b> че́й-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:опыт.html>о́пыт</a> (чьи́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:метода.html>методы</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perenjátʹ</b> čéj-libo ópyt (čʹí-libo metody)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to adopt smb's practices / methods</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переодевание.html>переодева́ние</a> (30155)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">переодева́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pereodevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переодевание.html>переодева́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereodevánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переодевание.html>переодева́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переодевание.html>переодева́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переодевание.html>переодева́ний</a></b>)

***переодеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переодеть.html>переоде́ть</a> (21364)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одеть.html>оде́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переодеть.html>переоде́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereodétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">переодева́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to change someone's clothes
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переодеть.html>переоде́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:девочка.html>де́вочку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бе́лое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:платье.html>пла́тье</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oná <b>pereodéla</b> dévočku v béloje plátʹje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">she changed the girl's dress for a white one</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to disguise <i>(smb)</i></li>
<li>to change <i>(smth)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переодеть.html>переоде́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:платье.html>пла́тье</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:юбка.html>ю́бку</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pereodétʹ</b> plátʹje (júbku)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to change one's dress (skirt)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***переоценивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переоценивать.html>переоце́нивать</a> (26352)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценить.html>переоцени́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pereocenítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценивать.html>переоце́нивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereocénivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценить.html>переоцени́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to revalue, to reappraise
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценивать.html>переоце́нивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ценность.html>це́нности</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pereocénivatʹ</b> cénnosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to reappraise old values</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to overestimate, to overrate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценивать.html>переоце́нивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pereocénivatʹ</b> svoí síly</i> ― <span class="e-translation">overestimate/overrate one's abilities; bite off more than one can chew</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недооценивать.html>недооце́нивать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nedoocénivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***переоценить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переоценить.html>переоцени́ть</a> (25224)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оценить.html>оцени́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ocenítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценить.html>переоцени́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereocenítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценивать.html>переоце́нивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to revalue, to reappraise</li>
<li>to overestimate, to overrate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценить.html>переоцени́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pereocenítʹ</b> svoí síly</i> ― <span class="e-translation">overestimate/overrate one's abilities; bite off more than one can chew</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трудно.html>тру́дно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценить.html>переоцени́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:факт.html>фа́кта</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">trúdno <b>pereocenítʹ</b> značénije étovo fákta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the importance of this fact can scarcely be overestimated/exaggerated</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переоценка.html>переоце́нка</a> (25902)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценить.html>переоцени́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pereocenítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценка.html>переоце́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereocénka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценка.html>переоце́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценка.html>переоце́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценка.html>переоце́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>revaluation, reappraisal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценка.html>переоце́нка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ценность.html>це́нностей</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pereocénka cénnostej</i> ― <span class="e-translation">reappraisal of values</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>overestimation</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">перепад-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perepad-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перепадать.html>перепада́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perepadátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перепасть.html>перепа́сть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fall to (someone's) lot, to become (someone's) responsibility <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ dative of person whose responsibility it is</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fall <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of intermittent rain, snow, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to subside</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pass by</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">folk  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lose weight, to get thin</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перепасть.html>перепа́сть</a> (23953)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pastʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перепасть.html>перепа́сть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perepástʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перепадать.html>перепада́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fall to (someone's) lot, to become (someone's) responsibility <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ dative of person whose responsibility it is</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fall <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of intermittent rain, snow, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to subside</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pass by</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">folk  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lose weight, to get thin</li></ol>

<tbody><tr>

***переписать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переписать.html>переписа́ть</a> (8284)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переписать.html>переписа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perepisátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переписывать.html>перепи́сывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rewrite, to retype
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переписать.html>переписа́ть</a></b> на́бело</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perepisátʹ</b> nábelo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make a fair copy (of); write out fair</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to copy</li>
<li>to make a list, to take a census <i>(of)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переписать.html>переписа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всех</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perepisátʹ</b> vsex</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take down (register) everybody's names</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to reregister
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переписать.html>переписа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perepisátʹ</b> dom na sebjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to reregister a house to one's own name</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***переписывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переписывать.html>перепи́сывать</a> (10792)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переписать.html>переписа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perepisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переписывать.html>перепи́сывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perepísyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переписать.html>переписа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rewrite, to retype
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переписывать.html>перепи́сывать</a></b> на́бело</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perepísyvatʹ</b> nábelo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make a fair copy (of); write out fair</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to copy</li>
<li>to make a list, to take a census <i>(of)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переписывать.html>перепи́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всех</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perepísyvatʹ</b> vsex</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take down (register) everybody's names</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to reregister
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переписывать.html>перепи́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perepísyvatʹ</b> dom na sebjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to reregister a house to one's own name</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
